pse_effect_access_ui_from_short_window = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = country
		has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_power_text_title
		custom_tooltip = pse_power_text_icon_desc
	}
}

pse_effect_access_ui_from_short = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = country
		has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = edict_pse_psi_ruler_ui_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pse.1000
			}
		}
	}
}

pse_effect_top_bar_switch = {
	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_top_bar_switch_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
			}
			else = {
				remove_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
			}
		}
	}
}

pse_effect_top_bar_switch_top_bar = {
	potential = {
		is_scope_type = country
		has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_top_bar_switch_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
			}
			else = {
				remove_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
			}
		}
	}
}

pse_effect_notify = {
	potential = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		}
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_notify_enable_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		}
	}
}

pse_effect_notify_enabled = {
	potential = {
		has_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_notify_disable_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		}
	}
}

pse_effect_notify_top_bar = {
	potential = {
        is_scope_type = country
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		}
		has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_notify_enable_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		}
	}
}

pse_effect_notify_enabled_top_bar = {
	potential = {
        is_scope_type = country
		has_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		has_country_flag = pse_top_bar_enabled
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_notify_disable_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_flag = pse_notify_enabled
		}
	}
}

pse_desc_effect_text = {
	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		change_variable = {
			which = pse_power
			value = 50
		}
		country_event = {
			#Calc require power cost
			id = pse.2004
		}
	}
}

pse_close_window_effect = {
	#CLEAR ALL variable for avoiding calc bug
	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	allow = {
	}
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				#Reset zro calc
				id = pse.1999
			}
			country_event = {
				#Deselect main
				id = pse.2002
			}
			country_event = {
				#Deselect power
				id = pse.2003
			}
			country_event = {
				#Calc require power cost reset
				id = pse.2005
			}
		}
	}
}

pse_power_main_button_effect_chosen_convenant = {
	potential = {
		leader = {
			OR = {
				has_trait = leader_trait_instrument_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_composer_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_eater_chosen
				has_trait = leader_trait_whisperers_chosen
			}
			NOT = {
				has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_chosen_covenant_desc
		custom_tooltip = pse_power_main_botton_effect_chosen_title
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = pse_power_botton_chosen_shroud_upset
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_shroud_nevermind
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_chosen_covenant_desc
		custom_tooltip = pse_power_main_botton_effect_chosen_title
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				#Reset zro calc
				id = pse.1999
			}
			country_event = {
				#Deselect main
				id = pse.2002
			}
			country_event = {
				#Deselect power
				id = pse.2003
			}
			country_event = {
				#Calc require power cost reset
				id = pse.2005
			}
			set_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_main_selected
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_main_selected

			has_country_flag = pse_power_cleanse_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_summon_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_combat_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_break_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_galaxy_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_covenant_knowledge_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_covenant_desire_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_covenant_eater_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_covenant_composer_main_selected
		}
	}

	}

	}
}

			has_country_flag = pse_power_summon_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_combat_main_selected
			has_country_flag = pse_power_break_main_selected

	}

	}
	effect = {
	}
}

###LEADER POWER###
    pse_power_botton_leader_find_button_effect = {
        #cost 35
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_main_selected
        }
        allow = {
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_leader_find_title
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_leader_find_desc
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_selected_tooltip
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_selected
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                #More intuitive visual
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_not_enough_power_and_zro_to_cast
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_power
                    value >= 18
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_leader_find_cant_fine_one
                any_owned_leader = {
                    species = {
                        OR = {
                            has_trait = trait_latent_psionic
                            has_trait = trait_psionic
                        }
                    }
                    NOT = {
                        OR = {
                            has_trait = leader_trait_psionic
                            has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_instrument_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_composer_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_eater_chosen
                            has_trait = leader_trait_whisperers_chosen
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            hidden_trigger = {
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown
                }
            }
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown
                }
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_360
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_360_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_720
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_720_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1080
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1080_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1440
                    }
                    custom_tooltip = pse_power_cooldown_1440_5year_desc
                }
                else_if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_country_flag = pse_power_leader_find_cooldown_1470
                    }

###BREAK###
    pse_power_botton_break_unity_button_effect = {
        #cost 115
        potential = {
            has_country_flag = pse_power_break_main_selected
        }
        allow = {
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_break_unity_title
            custom_tooltip = pse_power_botton_break_unity_desc
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_selected_tooltip
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_break_unity_selected
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                #More intuitive visual
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_not_enough_power_and_zro_to_cast
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_power
                    value >= 70
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_botton_break_dont_have_vaild_neighbor
                any_neighbor_country = {
                    has_communications = root
                    OR = {
                        is_berserker_to = root
                        is_belligerent_to = root
                        is_angry_to = root
                        is_domineering_to = root
                        is_unfriendly_to = root
                        is_hostile_to = root
                        is_rival = root
                        is_harming_relations_with = root
                        is_at_war_with = root
                    }
                    NOT = {
                        is_same_empire = root
                    }
                }
            }

pse_use_zro_discount_calc_plus = {
	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_zro_discount_plus_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = pse_select_power_text_select_one_of_them_first
			has_country_flag = pse_power_selected_one_of_them
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = pse_zro_discount_maxed
			check_variable = {
				which = pse_zro_discount_count
				value < 3
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = pse_power_botton_cleanse_cannot_use_zro
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = pse_power_cleanse_main_selected
			}
		}
		has_technology = tech_pse_zro_1
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = pse_zro_discount_plus_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = pse_zro_discount_count
				value = 1
			}
			country_event = {
				#Zro discount calc
				id = pse.2001
			}
		}
	}
}

	potential = {
		always = yes
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			success_text = PSE_COST_POWER_VARI_TEXT
			has_country_flag = pse_power_selected_one_of_them
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = pse_select_power_text_select_one_of_them_first
			has_country_flag = pse_power_selected_one_of_them
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = PSE_COST_POWER_REQUIRED_TOOLTIP
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = pse_power_text_message
					value > 0
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = pse_zro_cost_less_power_number
					value = 1
				}
			}

				resource = sr_zro
				value > 10

		}

			limit = {
				check_variable = {

###PSE CORRUPTION TOP BAR ABOVE###
###PSE MONTHLY POWER NUM
    pse_monthly_power_num_tooltip = {
        potential = {
            always = yes
        }
        allow = {
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_increase_month_desc
                always = no
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                fail_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_base
                always = no
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_hive_mind
                has_authority = auth_hive_mind
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler1
                leader = {
                    is_ruler = yes
                    pse_leader_is_psionic = no
                    species = {
                        has_trait = trait_latent_psionic
                        NOT = {
                            has_trait = trait_psionic
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler2
                leader = {
                    is_ruler = yes
                    has_trait = leader_trait_psionic
                    NOR = {
                        has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_instrument_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_composer_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_eater_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_whisperers_chosen
                    }
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler3
                leader = {
                    is_ruler = yes
                    NOT = {
                        has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
                    }
                    OR = {
                        has_trait = leader_trait_instrument_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_composer_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_eater_chosen
                        has_trait = leader_trait_whisperers_chosen
                    }
                }
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_shroud_nevermind
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_ruler4
                leader = {
                    is_ruler = yes
                    has_trait = leader_trait_chosen
                }
                NOT = {
                    has_country_flag = pse_power_chosen_shroud_nevermind
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader1
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 4
                }
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value < 10
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader2
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 9
                }
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value < 15
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader3
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 14
                }
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value < 20
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_leader4
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_leader_num
                    value > 19
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job1
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 3
                }
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value < 8
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job2
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 7
                }
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value < 12
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job3
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 11
                }
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value < 16
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_job4
                num_assigned_jobs = {
                    job = telepath
                    value > 15
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_tech1
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_1
                NOR = {
                    has_technology = tech_pse_power_2
                    has_technology = tech_pse_power_3
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_tech2
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_1
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_2
                NOT = {
                    has_technology = tech_pse_power_3
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_tech3
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_1
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_2
                has_technology = tech_pse_power_3
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_psy_siphon1
                has_global_flag = gigastructures_enabled
                OR = {
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_1
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_2
                }
                NOR = {
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3_aeternum
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_psy_siphon2
                has_global_flag = gigastructures_enabled
                OR = {
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3
                    has_megastructure = psychic_hypersiphon_3_aeternum
                }
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_edict
                has_edict = pse_psi_power
            }
            custom_tooltip = {
                success_text = pse_power_increase_month_modifier_zero_corruption
                has_technology = tech_pse_circle_1
                check_variable = {
                    which = pse_corruption
                    value < 1
                }
            }
        }
        effect = {
        }
    }
